## Diagram 1

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start[Input: rows, cfg] --> GroupByBOL[Group rows by BOL]
    GroupByBOL --> ProcessEachBOL[For each BOL group]
    ProcessEachBOL --> ComputeCounts[compute_counts]
    ComputeCounts --> CountLifecycles[Count lifecycle states]
    ComputeCounts --> CountETAs[Count ETAs from allowed statuses]
    CountLifecycles --> DecideLifecycle[_decide_lifecycle]
    DecideLifecycle --> CheckMajority{Has majority?}
    CheckMajority -->|Yes| UseMajority[Use majority lifecycle]
    CheckMajority -->|No| UseWaterfall[Use waterfall priority]
    UseMajority --> LifecycleDecided[Lifecycle decided]
    UseWaterfall --> LifecycleDecided
    LifecycleDecided --> CheckIfETAAllowed{Is lifecycle in statuses_using_eta?}
    CheckIfETAAllowed -->|Yes| SelectETA[_select_eta from counter]
    CheckIfETAAllowed -->|No| UseMapping[Use lifecycle_to_eta_value mapping]
    SelectETA --> ETAStrategy{eta_strategy?}
    ETAStrategy -->|MOST_FREQUENT| MostFrequent[Most frequent ETA]
    ETAStrategy -->|LATEST| Latest[Latest ETA]
    ETAStrategy -->|EARLIEST| Earliest[Earliest ETA]
    MostFrequent --> TieBreak{Tie?}
    TieBreak -->|Yes| UseFurthest[Use furthest timestamp]
    TieBreak -->|No| ETAChosen[ETA chosen]
    UseFurthest --> ETAChosen
    Latest --> ETAChosen
    Earliest --> ETAChosen
    UseMapping --> MapResult{Mapping result}
    MapResult --> ETAChosen
    ETAChosen --> CreateResult[Create BOL status result]
    CreateResult --> MoreBOLs{More BOLs?}
    MoreBOLs -->|Yes| ProcessEachBOL
    MoreBOLs -->|No| Return[Return results list]
```

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class BillOfLadingSearchBusinessLogic {
        +load_config() Cfg
        +compute_bol_status(rows, cfg) List~Result~
        +compute_counts(rows, cfg) Tuple
        -_decide_lifecycle(counter, total, cfg) str
        -_select_eta(counter, cfg) datetime
    }
    class BillOfLadingSearchConfiguration {
        +eta_strategy str
        +statuses_using_eta Tuple
        +lifecycle_priority List
        +lifecycle_to_eta_value Dict
        +threshold_percentage float
    }
    class FakeRow {
        +bill_of_lading str
        +lifecycle_state str
        +effective_destination_eta datetime|str|None
    }
    class PackageContainerStatus {
        +CREATED_STATE str
        +INROUTE_STATE str
        +DELAYED_STATE str
        +DELIVERED_STATE str
    }
    BillOfLadingSearchBusinessLogic --> BillOfLadingSearchConfiguration
    BillOfLadingSearchBusinessLogic --> FakeRow
    BillOfLadingSearchBusinessLogic --> PackageContainerStatus
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> AnalyzeRows
    AnalyzeRows --> CountStates: Group by BOL
    CountStates --> DecideLifecycle: Count lifecycle states & ETAs
    DecideLifecycle --> MajorityFound: Check for majority
    DecideLifecycle --> WaterfallPriority: No majority
    MajorityFound --> CheckETAEligibility
    WaterfallPriority --> CheckETAEligibility
    CheckETAEligibility --> SelectFromCounter: Lifecycle uses ETA selection
    CheckETAEligibility --> UseMapping: Lifecycle uses static mapping
    SelectFromCounter --> ApplyStrategy
    ApplyStrategy --> MostFrequent: Strategy = MOST_FREQUENT
    ApplyStrategy --> LatestDate: Strategy = LATEST
    ApplyStrategy --> EarliestDate: Strategy = EARLIEST
    MostFrequent --> ResultReady
    LatestDate --> ResultReady
    EarliestDate --> ResultReady
    UseMapping --> MapToValue: DELIVERED→None, DELAYED→"tbd", CREATED→"tbd"
    MapToValue --> ResultReady
    ResultReady --> [*]
```
